;----------------------------------------------------------
;------  Traits: AI Boost  --------------------------------;boost traits for all AI characters
;------  Traits: Character Unique  ------------------------;biographies
;------  Traits: Ethnicity  -------------------------------;every general should have all of the appropriate race and sub-race traits
;------  Traits: Hero Abilities  --------------------------
;------  Traits: Faction Leadership and Succession  -------;faction leader and heir succession related traits
;------  Traits: Scripts  ---------------------------------;traits tied to campaign_script
;------  Traits: Agents  ----------------------------------;traits related to admirals, spies and diplomats
;------  Traits: Chivalry  --------------------------------;chivalry attribute mechanics
;------  Traits: Militaristic  ----------------------------;shared combat and other military related traits
;------  Traits: Hates & Fears Faction  -------------------
;------  Traits: Settlement Conqueror  --------------------;traits for conquering certain settlements
;------  Traits: Governance & Economy  --------------------
;------  Traits: Personality & Lifestyle  -----------------;traits representing personalities and lifestyles
;------  Traits: Faction Specific Traits & Mechanics  -----;faction or culture unique traits and special mechanics
;------  Traits: Ancillary Tied or Dependant  -------------;traits dependant on ancillaries or tied to them
;----------------------------------------------------------
;
;

Trigger AIBoost_Add1
    WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

    Condition IsFactionAIControlled
        and IsGeneral
        and Trait AIBoost = 0

    Affects AIBoost 1 Chance 100
;----------------------------------------------------------
Trigger RingInfluence_add_orcs
    WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

    Condition CharacterReligion catholic
        and not FactionType gundabad
        and not FactionType france
        and IsGeneral
        and I_EventCounter sauron_ai > 0
        and Trait RingInfluence < 1

    Affects RingInfluence 1 Chance 100
;----------------------------------------------------------
Trigger RingInfluence_add_men
    WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

    Condition CharacterReligion orthodox
        and IsGeneral
        and I_EventCounter sauron_ai > 0
        and Trait RingInfluence < 1

    Affects RingInfluence 1 Chance 100
;----------------------------------------------------------
Trigger RingInfluence_remove
    WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

    Condition Trait RingInfluence > 0
        and I_EventCounter sauron_ai < 1

    Affects RingInfluence -1 Chance 100

;------  Triggers: Faction Leadership and Succession  -----
;----------------------------------------------------------
Trigger NotAFactionLeader
    WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

    Condition IsGeneral
        and not IsFactionLeader
        and Trait NotFactionLeader < 1

    Affects NotFactionLeader 1 Chance  100
;----------------------------------------------------------
Trigger IsNowFactionLeader
    WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

    Condition IsGeneral
        and IsFactionLeader
        and Trait NotFactionLeader > 0

    Affects BecameFactionLeader 1 Chance  100
    Affects NotFactionLeader -1 Chance  100
;----------------------------------------------------------
Trigger NextHeirTrait_trigger1
    WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

    Condition FactionIsLocal
        and IsGeneral
        and Trait NextHeirTrait = 0
        and HasAncType NextHeir
        and not IsFactionLeader
        and not IsFactionHeir

    Affects NextHeirTrait  1  Chance  100
;----------------------------------------------------------
Trigger NextHeirTrait_trigger2
    WhenToTest CharacterTurnStart

    Condition FactionIsLocal
        and Trait NextHeirTrait = 1
        and not HasAncType NextHeir

    Affects NextHeirTrait  -1  Chance  100
;----------------------------------------------------------
Trigger NextHeirTrait_trigger3
    WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

    Condition Trait NextHeirTrait == 1
        and Trait BecameFactionLeader > 0

    Affects NextHeirTrait  -1  Chance  100
;----------------------------------------------------------
Trigger BecomesHeir
    WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

    Condition IsFactionHeir
        and Trait FactionHeir = 0
        and Trait FactionHeirCustom = 0
        and Trait CustomBG = 0
        and Trait NazgulRace = 0


    Affects FactionHeir 1 Chance 100
;----------------------------------------------------------
Trigger BecomesHeirCustom1
    WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

    Condition IsFactionHeir
        and Trait FactionHeir = 0
        and Trait FactionHeirCustom = 0
        and Trait CustomBG = 1
        and Trait NazgulRace = 0 ;temporary TBD

    Affects FactionHeirCustom 1 Chance 100
;----------------------------------------------------------
;temporary TBD
Trigger BecomesHeirCustom2
    WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

    Condition IsFactionHeir
        and Trait FactionHeir = 0
        and Trait FactionHeirCustom = 0
        and Trait NazgulRace = 1

    Affects FactionHeirCustom 1 Chance 100
;----------------------------------------------------------
Trigger BecomesLeader_All
    WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

    Condition Trait BecameFactionLeader > 0
        and Trait CustomBG = 0

    Affects FactionHeir -1 Chance 100
    Affects FactionLeader 1 Chance 100
;----------------------------------------------------------
Trigger BecomesLeader_Mordor
    WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

    Condition Trait FactionLeader > 0
        and FactionType England
        and Trait FactionLeaderCustom = 0
        
    Affects FactionLeaderCustom 1 Chance 100
;----------------------------------------------------------
Trigger BecomesLeader_Custom
    WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

    Condition Trait FactionLeader = 0
        and Trait BecameFactionLeader > 0
        and Trait CustomBG = 1

    Affects FactionHeirCustom -1 Chance 100
    Affects FactionLeaderCustom 1 Chance 100
;----------------------------------------------------------
;temporary until script fixed TBD
Trigger BecomesLeader_CustomNazguls
    WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

    Condition Trait FactionLeader = 0
        and Trait BecameFactionLeader > 0
        and Trait FactionLeaderCustom = 0
        and Trait NazgulRace = 1

    Affects FactionHeir -1 Chance 100
    Affects FactionLeaderCustom 1 Chance 100
;----------------------------------------------------------
;IMPORTANT: this trigger must always be placed after all other succession triggers

Trigger BecomingFactionLeaderFinished
    WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

    Condition IsGeneral
        and Trait BecameFactionLeader > 0

    Affects BecameFactionLeader -1 Chance 100

    Affects Corrupt 1 Chance 8
    Affects DeceiverVirtue 1 Chance 8
    Affects Unjust 1 Chance 8

Trigger Admiral_initiation1
    WhenToTest PostBattle
    Condition AgentType = admiral
        and WonBattle
        and Trait Sailor = 0
        and Trait CheckAdmiral = 0

    Affects CheckAdmiral 1 Chance 100
    Affects Sailor 6 Chance 100
;----------------------------------------------------------
Trigger Admiral_initiation2
    WhenToTest PostBattle
    Condition AgentType = admiral
        and not WonBattle
        and Trait Sailor = 0
        and Trait CheckAdmiral = 0

    Affects CheckAdmiral 1 Chance 100
    Affects Sailor 5 Chance 100
;----------------------------------------------------------

        and not FactionType aztecs

        and GeneralFoughtInCombat
        and BattleOdds <= 0.75

        and GeneralFoughtInCombat
        and BattleOdds <= 0.75

        and not FactionType turks
        and not FactionType teutonic_order
        and Trait StrategyChivalryGood > 0
        and Trait FearGeneral = 0
        and not TargetReligion catholic

    Affects Authoritarian  1  Chance  10
    Affects BadDisciplinarian 1 Chance 30
    Affects StrategyChivalryGood -1 Chance 40
;----------------------------------------------------------

    WhenToTest OccupySettlement

    Condition IsGeneral
        and FactionCultureType eastern_european

    WhenToTest GeneralCaptureSettlement

    Condition SettlementName Morgul_Vale
        and CharacterReligion islam
        and Trait SettlementConqueror < 1

    Affects MinasIthilLiberator 2 Chance 100
    Affects SettlementConqueror 1 Chance 100
;----------------------------------------------------------

    WhenToTest GeneralCaptureSettlement

    Condition SettlementName Morgul_Vale
        and CharacterReligion islam
        and Trait SettlementConqueror > 0
        and not Trait MinasIthilLiberator > 0

    Affects MinasIthilLiberator 1 Chance 100

        and not CultureType eastern_european
        and not CultureType gondor
        and not FactionType turks
        and Trait SettlementConqueror < 1

    Affects MinasIthilConqueror 2 Chance 100
    Affects SettlementConqueror 1 Chance 100

    Affects MinasIthilConqueror 1 Chance 100

        and not CultureType eastern_european

;##########################################################
;----------------------------------------------------------
;------  Triggers: Governance & Economy  ------------------
;----------------------------------------------------------
Trigger Governor_Check_Add_Player
    WhenToTest CharacterTurnEndInSettlement

    Condition not IsFactionAIControlled
        and IsGeneral
        and TimeInRegion > 3
        and RemainingMPPercentage = 100
        and Trait NazgulRace = 0
        and Trait WraithRace = 0
        and Trait KingDead = 0
        and Trait Sauron = 0
        and Trait GovernorCheck = 0
        and Trait GovernorLock = 0

    Affects GovernorCheck 1 Chance 100
    Affects GovernorLock 1 Chance 100
;----------------------------------------------------------
Trigger Governor_Check_Remove_Player
    WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

    Condition not IsFactionAIControlled
        and IsGeneral
        and not EndedInSettlement
        and Trait NazgulRace = 0
        and Trait WraithRace = 0
        and Trait KingDead = 0
        and Trait Sauron = 0
        and Trait GovernorCheck = 1
        and Trait GovernorLock = 1

    Affects GovernorCheck -1 Chance 100
    Affects GovernorLock -1 Chance 100
;----------------------------------------------------------
Trigger Governor_Check_Add_AI
    WhenToTest CharacterTurnEndInSettlement

    Condition IsFactionAIControlled
        and IsGeneral
        and TimeInRegion > 3
        and Trait NazgulRace = 0
        and Trait WraithRace = 0
        and Trait KingDead = 0
        and Trait Sauron = 0
        and Trait GovernorCheck = 0

    Affects GovernorCheck 1 Chance 100
;----------------------------------------------------------
Trigger Governor_Check_Remove_AI
    WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

    Condition IsFactionAIControlled
        and IsGeneral
        and not EndedInSettlement
        and Trait NazgulRace = 0
        and Trait WraithRace = 0
        and Trait KingDead = 0
        and Trait Sauron = 0
        and Trait GovernorCheck = 1

    Affects GovernorCheck -1 Chance 100
;----------------------------------------------------------
Trigger GoodAdministrator_Add_Good
    WhenToTest GovernorUnitTrained

    Condition GovernorTaxLevel >= tax_high
        and Trait NazgulRace = 0
        and Trait WraithRace = 0
        and Trait KingDead = 0
        and Trait Sauron = 0
        and Trait BadAdministrator < 1

    Affects GoodAdministrator 1 Chance 4
    Affects Recruiter 1 Chance 8
;----------------------------------------------------------
Trigger GoodAdministrator_Add_Bad
    WhenToTest GovernorUnitTrained

    Condition GovernorTaxLevel >= tax_high
        and Trait NazgulRace = 0
        and Trait WraithRace = 0
        and Trait KingDead = 0
        and Trait Sauron = 0
        and Trait BadAdministrator > 0

    Affects BadAdministrator -1 Chance 15
    Affects Recruiter 1 Chance 8
;----------------------------------------------------------
Trigger GoodAdministrator_Add2
    WhenToTest GovernorUnitTrained

    Condition GovernorTaxLevel >= tax_high
        and Trait GovernorCheck = 1
        and Trait NazgulRace = 0
        and Trait WraithRace = 0
        and Trait KingDead = 0
        and Trait Sauron = 0

    Affects GoodAdministrator 1 Chance 6
    Affects Recruiter 1 Chance 8
;----------------------------------------------------------
Trigger BadAdministrator_Add1
    WhenToTest GovernorCityRebels

    Condition GovernorTaxLevel >= tax_high
        and Trait EntsRace = 0
        and Trait NazgulRace = 0
        and Trait WraithRace = 0
        and Trait KingDead = 0
        and Trait Sauron = 0
        and Trait Hero = 0

    Affects BadAdministrator 1 Chance 100
;----------------------------------------------------------
Trigger BadAdministrator_Add2
    WhenToTest GovernorCityRiots

    Condition GovernorTaxLevel >= tax_high
        and Trait EntsRace = 0
        and Trait NazgulRace = 0
        and Trait WraithRace = 0
        and Trait KingDead = 0
        and Trait Sauron = 0
        and Trait Hero = 0

    Affects BadAdministrator 1 Chance 40
;----------------------------------------------------------
Trigger BadAdministrator_Add3
    WhenToTest GovernorBuildingCompleted

    Condition GovernorLoyaltyLevel <= loyalty_disillusioned
        and GovernorTaxLevel >= tax_high
        and Trait Hero = 0
        and Trait NazgulRace = 0
        and Trait WraithRace = 0
        and Trait KingDead = 0
        and Trait Sauron = 0

    Affects BadAdministrator 1 Chance 10
;----------------------------------------------------------
Trigger Government_GovernorUnitTrained_Tax
    WhenToTest GovernorUnitTrained

    Condition GovernorLoyaltyLevel >= loyalty_disillusioned
        and GovernorTaxLevel = tax_extortionate
        and Trait NazgulRace = 0
        and Trait WraithRace = 0
        and Trait KingDead = 0
        and Trait Sauron = 0

    Affects GoodTaxman 1 Chance 5
;----------------------------------------------------------
Trigger Government_BuildingCompleted1
    WhenToTest GovernorBuildingCompleted

    Condition GovernorLoyaltyLevel >= loyalty_disillusioned
        and GovernorTaxLevel = tax_extortionate
        and Trait NazgulRace = 0
        and Trait WraithRace = 0
        and Trait KingDead = 0
        and Trait Sauron = 0

    Affects GoodAdministrator 1 Chance 5
    Affects GoodTaxman 1 Chance 50
;----------------------------------------------------------

Trigger Unlock_Nazgul_For_player_gondor
    WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

    Condition FactionType england
        and I_IsFactionAIControlled england
        and not I_IsFactionAIControlled sicily
        and IsGeneral
        and Trait NazgulLocked = 1

    Affects NazgulLocked -1 Chance 100
;----------------------------------------------------------

    Condition FactionType england
        and I_IsFactionAIControlled england
        and I_IsFactionAIControlled sicily
        and I_TurnNumber > 9
        and IsGeneral
        and Trait Nazgul = 8
        and Trait NazgulLocked = 1

    Affects NazgulLocked -1 Chance 100

;------  Wounds, Injuries  --------------------------------
;----------------------------------------------------------
Trigger General_Wounded_Add1
    WhenToTest PostBattle

    Condition not IsFactionAIControlled
        and GeneralHPLostRatioinBattle > 0.3
		and GeneralHPLostRatioinBattle < 0.75
		and Trait Wounded = 0

    Affects Wounded 2 Chance 25
;----------------------------------------------------------
Trigger General_Wounded_Add2
    WhenToTest PostBattle

    Condition not IsFactionAIControlled
        and GeneralHPLostRatioinBattle > 0.75
		and Trait Wounded = 0

    Affects Wounded 3 Chance 33
;----------------------------------------------------------
Trigger General_Wounded_Remove
    WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

    Condition not IsFactionAIControlled
        and IsGeneral
        and Trait Wounded > 0

    Affects Wounded -1 Chance 100
	Affects Wounded -1 Chance 25
	Affects Wounded -1 Chance 10
;----------------------------------------------------------
Trigger General_Wounded_Injury1
    WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

    Condition not IsFactionAIControlled
        and IsGeneral
        and Trait Wounded > 1
        and Trait BattleScarred > 2

    Affects Maimed 1 Chance 3
    Affects OneEyed 1 Chance 3
    Affects OneHanded 1 Chance 3
    Affects OneLegged 1 Chance 3
;----------------------------------------------------------
Trigger General_Wounded_Injury2
    WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

    Condition not IsFactionAIControlled
        and CultureType eastern_european
        and IsGeneral
        and Trait Wounded > 1
        and Trait BattleScarred > 2

    Affects Disfigured 1 Chance 3
;----------------------------------------------------------
Trigger General_Wounded_Injury3
    WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

    Condition not IsFactionAIControlled
        and CultureType southern_european
        and IsGeneral
        and Trait Wounded > 1
        and Trait BattleScarred > 2

    Affects AxeInTheHead 1 Chance 3
;----------------------------------------------------------

Trigger Eregion_Guild_Add
    WhenToTest CharacterTurnEndInSettlement

    Condition SettlementName Eregion
        and CultureType greek
        and SettlementBuildingExists = m_gwaith_i_mirdain_guild
        and IsGeneral
        and Trait GovernorCheck = 1
        and Trait EregionGuild = 0

    Affects EregionGuild 2 Chance 100
;----------------------------------------------------------

    WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

        and CultureType greek
        and IsGeneral

Trigger Brave_Coward_Trigger
    WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

    Condition Trait Brave > 0
        and Trait Coward > 0

    Affects Brave -1  Chance 100
    Affects Coward -1  Chance 100
;----------------------------------------------------------
Trigger Energetic_Slothful_Trigger
    WhenToTest CharacterTurnEnd

    Condition Trait Energetic > 0
        and Trait Slothful > 0

    Affects Energetic -1  Chance 100
    Affects Slothful -1  Chance 100

Trigger NoGateSpy
 WhenToTest SpyMission

 Condition AgentType = spy
    and MissionSuccessLevel > not_successful
    
       
 Affects NoGate 1 Chance 100 
;----------------------------------------------------------
Trigger NoGateSpy_Removal
 WhenToTest CharacterSelected

 Condition AgentType = spy
        and Trait NoGate = 1
        and not EndedInSettlement

       
 Affects NoGate -1 Chance 100
